REFERENCE  (J,NST,35,851,1998)   Main reference, graphs are given 22354  1   12 
           ((S,JAERI-C-96-008,231,1996)=                          22354  1   13 
           (S,INDC(JPN)-175,231,1996))    Proceedings of the      22354  1   14

REL-REF    (M,22309001,N.Ito+,J,NIM/A,337,474,1994)  Experim.     22354  1   17 
                  and analysis details                            22354  1   18 
METHOD     (ASSOP) Detection of alpha particles                   22354  1   19 
DETECTOR   (IOCH)  High pressure gridded ionization chamber       22354  1   20 
             krypton with admixtures of C-O2 or C-H4 were used    22354  1   21 
             as counting gases -                                  22354  1   22 
             Kr+C-O2(3%) for (n,p) reaction;                      22354  1   23 
             Kr+C-H4(5%) for (n,alpha) reaction (4 - 10.6 MeV);   22354  1   24 
             Kr+C-O2(2%) for (n,alpha) reaction (14 MeV).         22354  1   25 
           (SIBAR) The neutron flux on the sample was measured    22354  1   26 
           using a proton recoil counter consisting of a 20.mu-m  22354  1   27 
           thick polypropylene radiator and a silicon surface     22354  1   28 
           barrier detector (300 mm2 sensitive area and 500. mu-m 22354  1   29 
           thick) in a vacuum chamber.                            22354  1   30 
           (SCIN) Neutron intensity was monitored with two NE213  22354  1   31 
           scintillators placed at the 0. and 900. degr.          22354  1   32 
           direction.                                             22354  1   33 
FACILITY   (DYNAM,2JPNTOH) Tohoku Univ.Dynamitron accelerator for 22354  1   34 
             production of 4 - 6.5 and 14 MeV neutrons            22354  1   35 
           (VDGT,2JPNJAE) JAERI tandem accelerator for            22354  1   36 
             production of 6.5 - 10.6 MeV neutrons                22354  1   37 
INC-SOURCE (D-D) For 4 - 10 MeV neutron production                22354  1   38 
           (D-T) For 14 MeV neutron production                    22354  1   39 
MONITOR    (1-H-1(N,EL)1-H-1,,SIG)   Recoil proton detection      22354  1   40 
             Determination of absolute values based on the        22354  1   41 
             neutron flux and the number of sample atoms          22354  1   42 
ANALYSIS   Double differential cross sections were obtained by the22354  1   43 
           following procedure:                                   22354  1   44 
             (i) energy calibration using a 241Am alpha source,   22354  1   45 
             (ii) deduction of energy spectra for the emission    22354  1   46 
             angle (cosine) according to Eqs. given in NST,35,851 22354  1   47 
             (iii) elimination of low energy background protons,  22354  1   48 
             (iv) correction for the energy loss of               22354  1   49 
              alpha-particles in the sample,                      22354  1   50 
             (v) determination of absolute values based on the    22354  1   51 
             neutron flux and the number of sample atoms.         22354  1   52
